HTTPS is used to provide an additional layer of security when transferring data over the internet, ensuring that the data remains encrypted and protected from unauthorized access [7].

2024-11-08 12:19:33,767: ObserveEventsHandler(  207): MEASUREMENT: LLMChatEnd response: assistant: HTTP stands for HyperText Transfer Protocol. It is a fundamental protocol used for transferring data, including web pages, over the internet. HTTP is the foundation of the web, allowing different systems to communicate with each other and exchange information (Source 8). 

In web addresses, HTTP is often seen at the beginning of a URL, followed by "://" and then the domain name and path to a specific resource. For example, "http://www.example.com" is a URL that starts with the HTTP protocol (Source 9). 

It's worth noting that there's also a secure version of the protocol, HTTPS, which stands for HyperText Transfer Protocol Secure. HTTPS is used to provide an additional layer of security when transferring data over the internet, ensuring that the data remains encrypted and protected from unauthorized access (Source 10).
